 The bill was passed for the fourth time on March 30 amid protests in the Gujarat assembly
 tabhi se ise lekar gujarat main kai sanghathan iskaa virodh kar rahe hai

 lekin, ab ye khabar aa rahi he ki rajyapal ne is bill par apni manjuuri kii muhar laga di he or raashtrapati kii manjuuri ke liye grih mantralay ko bhej diya he
 This bill has again reached the President, it is important that two presidents have rejected this bill earlier due to the objectionable provisions of this bill
 is bill ke jin praavdhaanon ko lekar virodh he ve hai, police ke saamne diya gaya bayaan saboot mana ja saktaa he or use saboot ke taur par court main pesh bhi kiya ja saktaa he, police remand kii miyaad aam taur par 15 din tak kii hi hoti he jo iske tahat darj honevaale maamalon main 30 din tak kii ho sakati he
